NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICE
My daughter, S. Aparna, born on 2nd November 1993 was Legally Adopted by Thiru K. Manokaran and
Tmt. M. Vijaya, vide registered Adoption Deed bearing registration No. 2898 dated 17th March 1999, and her name was
changed to M. Aparna in all her school records.
Now the Adoption Notification stands cancelled as per the courts Judgement, pronounced vide O.S. No. 1898/2017
on 15th November 2017, and on its direction a deed of cancellation of Adoption was prepared and registered
with the Sub-Registrar office at Adyar vide Reg. No. 11835 dated 13th April 2018. As a result of this my daughter
shall henceforth be known as S. APARNA once again, with her residence at No. 20, Bajanai Koil Street, Pallipattu,
Taramani, Chennai-600 113.

Chennai,
2nd July 2018.

K. SANKARAN,
(Father)

ON BEHALF OF THE GOVERNMENT OF TAMIL NADU
